<a name='T-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor'></a>
## AutoCompleteEditor `type`

##### Namespace

CommunityToolkit.WinForms.FluentUI.Controls

##### Summary

A RichTextBox control with auto-complete and suggestion capabilities.

##### Remarks

This control extends the RichTextBox to provide auto-complete suggestions and command
  sending functionality. It includes various properties to customize the behavior and
  appearance of the suggestions.

The control uses a timer to manage the timing of suggestion requests and can display
  an overlay panel to indicate waiting states.

The [AcceptsTab](#P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-AcceptsTab 'CommunityToolkit.WinForms.FluentUI.Controls.AutoCompleteEditor.AcceptsTab') property is set to true by default, so the user can
  use Tab and Enter to edit, but needs to use Ctrl+Tab to navigate out of the Editor, and
  a Form's Default-Button cannot be triggered with Enter if a [AutoCompleteEditor](#T-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor 'CommunityToolkit.WinForms.FluentUI.Controls.AutoCompleteEditor')
  has the focus.

<a name='M-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-#ctor'></a>
### #ctor() `constructor`

##### Summary

Initializes a new instance of the [AutoCompleteEditor](#T-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor 'CommunityToolkit.WinForms.FluentUI.Controls.AutoCompleteEditor') class.

##### Parameters

This constructor has no parameters.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-AllowExistingRemainingTextReplacement'></a>
### AllowExistingRemainingTextReplacement `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets a value indicating whether to allow replacement of existing remaining text.

##### Remarks

This property determines whether the existing remaining text can be replaced by
  the auto-complete suggestions.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-AutoCorrectionColor'></a>
### AutoCorrectionColor `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the color for auto-corrections.

##### Remarks

This property defines the color used for displaying auto-corrections in the control.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-CorrectionCandidateColor'></a>
### CorrectionCandidateColor `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the color for correction candidates.

##### Remarks

This property defines the color used for displaying correction candidates in the
  control.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-CurrentParagraphSpan'></a>
### CurrentParagraphSpan `property`

##### Summary

Gets the current paragraph as a ReadOnlySpan<char> 
 based on the caret position.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-MaxRemainingCharsSuggestionRequestSensitivity'></a>
### MaxRemainingCharsSuggestionRequestSensitivity `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the maximum character count to trigger suggestion request.

##### Remarks

This property defines the maximum number of characters that can remain before
  a suggestion request is triggered.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-MinCharChangedBeforeNextTextReviewRequest'></a>
### MinCharChangedBeforeNextTextReviewRequest `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the minimum character changes before the next text review request.

##### Remarks

This property defines the minimum number of character changes that must occur
  before the next text review request is triggered.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-MinPrecedingCharsSuggestionRequestSensitivity'></a>
### MinPrecedingCharsSuggestionRequestSensitivity `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the minimum character count to trigger suggestion request.

##### Remarks

This property defines the minimum number of characters that must be typed before
  a suggestion request is triggered.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-MinTimeSuggestionRequestSensitivity'></a>
### MinTimeSuggestionRequestSensitivity `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the minimum time in seconds to trigger suggestion request.

##### Remarks

This property defines the minimum time in seconds that must pass before a
  suggestion request is triggered.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-MinTimeThresholdForNextTextReviewRequest'></a>
### MinTimeThresholdForNextTextReviewRequest `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the minimum time threshold for the next text review request.

##### Remarks

This property defines the minimum time in seconds that must pass before the next
  text review request is triggered.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-PrecedingParagraphSpan'></a>
### PrecedingParagraphSpan `property`

##### Summary

Gets the preceding paragraph text as a ReadOnlySpan<char> 
 before the caret position.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-RemainingParagraphSpan'></a>
### RemainingParagraphSpan `property`

##### Summary

Gets the remaining paragraph text as a ReadOnlySpan<char> 
 starting at the caret position.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-StandardEditColor'></a>
### StandardEditColor `property`

##### Summary

Gets or sets the color for standard text editing.

##### Remarks

This property defines the color used for standard text editing in the control.

<a name='P-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-SuggestionColor'></a>

<a name='M-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-EnsureOverlayInitialized'></a>

<a name='M-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-InitializeOverlay'></a>
### InitializeOverlay() `method`

##### Summary

Initializes the overlay panel.

##### Parameters

This method has no parameters.

##### Remarks

This method sets up the overlay panel that is used to indicate waiting states.
  The overlay panel is resized to match the size of the RichTextBox and is added
  to the control's collection of child controls.

<a name='M-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-AutoCompleteEditor-ShowSuggestion-System-String-'></a>
### ShowSuggestion(suggestionText) `method`

##### Summary

Inserts the EffectiveSymbolText with only the symbol part formatted as the symbol font,
superscripted, and using SuggestionColor, while the leading space uses the normal formatting.
Then inserts the suggestion text using SuggestionColor and the normal font, preserving the original selection.

##### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- |
| suggestionText | [System.String](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.String 'System.String') | The text of the suggestion to insert. |

<a name='T-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-ContentFreezePanel'></a>

<a name='M-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-ContentFreezePanel-#ctor'></a>

<a name='F-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Imaging-ImageFileInfo-s_propertyLookUp'></a>

## TypedFormatterComponent\`1 `type`

##### Namespace

CommunityToolkit.WinForms.FluentUI.Controls.TypedInputExtenders

##### Summary

Provides a base class for components that extend [TextBox](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.Windows.Forms.TextBox 'System.Windows.Forms.TextBox') controls with formatting capabilities
and value conversion for data entry purposes.

##### Generic Types

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| T | The type of the value being formatted and converted. |

<a name='M-CommunityToolkit-WinForms-FluentUI-Controls-TypedInputExtenders-TypedFormatterComponent`1-TryConvertToValueAsync-System-Windows-Forms-TextBox,System-String,System-Threading-CancellationToken-'></a>
### TryConvertToValueAsync(textBox,stringValue,token) `method`

##### Summary

Attempts to convert a string to a value and assign it to the specified [TextBox](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.Windows.Forms.TextBox 'System.Windows.Forms.TextBox').

##### Returns

`true` if the conversion succeeded and the value was assigned; otherwise, `false`.

##### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- |
| textBox | [System.Windows.Forms.TextBox](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.Windows.Forms.TextBox 'System.Windows.Forms.TextBox') | The [TextBox](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.Windows.Forms.TextBox 'System.Windows.Forms.TextBox') to set the value for. |
| stringValue | [System.String](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.String 'System.String') | The string to convert to a value. |
| token | [System.Threading.CancellationToken](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.Threading.CancellationToken 'System.Threading.CancellationToken') | A cancellation token that can be used to cancel the operation. |

desired value.

CallerMemberName. |
| actionOnValidate | [System.Func{System.Boolean}](http://msdn.microsoft.com/query/dev14.query?appId=Dev14IDEF1&l=EN-US&k=k:System.Func 'System.Func{System.Boolean}') | Action to execute when the validation succeeds. |
